function InitGlobals2 takes nothing returns nothing
	local integer i=0
	set i=0
	loop
		exitwhen(i>1)
		set udg_strings01[i]=""
		set udg_integers01[i]=0
		set udg_integers02[i]=0
		set udg_integers03[i]=0
		set udg_integers04[i]=0
		set udg_integers05[i]=0
		set udg_booleans01[i]=false
		set udg_integers06[i]=0
		set udg_units03[i]=null
		set udg_integers07[i]=0
		set udg_integers08[i]=0
		set udg_integers09[i]=0
		set udg_integers10[i]=0
		set udg_integers11[i]=0
		set udg_integers12[i]=0
		set udg_booleans02[i]=false
		set udg_integers13[i]=0
		set udg_integers14[i]=0
		set udg_integers15[i]=0
		set udg_integers16[i]=0
		set udg_integers17[i]=0
		set udg_integers18[i]=0
		set udg_booleans03[i]=false
		set udg_integers19[i]=0
		set udg_integers20[i]=0
		set udg_integers21[i]=0
		set udg_integers22[i]=0
		set udg_integers23[i]=0
		set udg_integers24[i]=0
		set udg_integers25[i]=0
		set udg_integers26[i]=0
		set udg_integers27[i]=0
		set udg_booleans04[i]=false
		set udg_integers28[i]=0
		set udg_integers29[i]=0
		set udg_integers31[i]=0
		set i=i+1
	endloop
	set udg_dialog01=DialogCreate()
	set udg_timer01=CreateTimer()
	set udg_force01=CreateForce()
	set udg_group01=CreateGroup()
	set udg_dialog02=DialogCreate()
	set udg_timer02=CreateTimer()
endfunction

function Trig_CF_Cast_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
	return(GetSpellAbilityId()=='A059')
endfunction

function Trig_CF_Cast_Func028A takes nothing returns nothing
	call SetUnitPathing(GetEnumUnit(),false)
	call UnitApplyTimedLifeBJ(10.,'BTLF',GetEnumUnit())
endfunction

function Trig_CF_Cast_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
	set udg_unit03=GetSpellAbilityUnit()
	set udg_real04=100.
	set udg_integer25=$A
	set udg_location02=GetSpellTargetLoc()
	set udg_real05=300.
	set udg_integer26='h01M'
	call AddSpecialEffectLocBJ(udg_location02,"Abilities\\Spells\\Human\\FlameStrike\\FlameStrikeTarget.mdl")
	set udg_effect01=bj_lastCreatedEffect
	call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1,udg_integer26,GetOwningPlayer(udg_unit03),PolarProjectionBJ(udg_location02,udg_real05,.0),bj_UNIT_FACING)
	call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1,udg_integer26,GetOwningPlayer(udg_unit03),PolarProjectionBJ(udg_location02,udg_real05,20.),bj_UNIT_FACING)
	call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1,udg_integer26,GetOwningPlayer(udg_unit03),PolarProjectionBJ(udg_location02,udg_real05,40.),bj_UNIT_FACING)
	call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1,udg_integer26,GetOwningPlayer(udg_unit03),PolarProjectionBJ(udg_location02,udg_real05,60.),bj_UNIT_FACING)
	call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1,udg_integer26,GetOwningPlayer(udg_unit03),PolarProjectionBJ(udg_location02,udg_real05,80.),bj_UNIT_FACING)
	call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1,udg_integer26,GetOwningPlayer(udg_unit03),PolarProjectionBJ(udg_location02,udg_real05,100.),bj_UNIT_FACING)
	call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1,udg_integer26,GetOwningPlayer(udg_unit03),PolarProjectionBJ(udg_location02,udg_real05,120.),bj_UNIT_FACING)
	call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1,udg_integer26,GetOwningPlayer(udg_unit03),PolarProjectionBJ(udg_location02,udg_real05,140.),bj_UNIT_FACING)
	call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1,udg_integer26,GetOwningPlayer(udg_unit03),PolarProjectionBJ(udg_location02,udg_real05,160.),bj_UNIT_FACING)
	call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1,udg_integer26,GetOwningPlayer(udg_unit03),PolarProjectionBJ(udg_location02,udg_real05,180.),bj_UNIT_FACING)
	call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1,udg_integer26,GetOwningPlayer(udg_unit03),PolarProjectionBJ(udg_location02,udg_real05,200.),bj_UNIT_FACING)
	call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1,udg_integer26,GetOwningPlayer(udg_unit03),PolarProjectionBJ(udg_location02,udg_real05,220.),bj_UNIT_FACING)
	call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1,udg_integer26,GetOwningPlayer(udg_unit03),PolarProjectionBJ(udg_location02,udg_real05,240.),bj_UNIT_FACING)
	call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1,udg_integer26,GetOwningPlayer(udg_unit03),PolarProjectionBJ(udg_location02,udg_real05,260.),bj_UNIT_FACING)
	call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1,udg_integer26,GetOwningPlayer(udg_unit03),PolarProjectionBJ(udg_location02,udg_real05,280.),bj_UNIT_FACING)
	call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1,udg_integer26,GetOwningPlayer(udg_unit03),PolarProjectionBJ(udg_location02,udg_real05,300.),bj_UNIT_FACING)
	call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1,udg_integer26,GetOwningPlayer(udg_unit03),PolarProjectionBJ(udg_location02,udg_real05,320.),bj_UNIT_FACING)
	call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1,udg_integer26,GetOwningPlayer(udg_unit03),PolarProjectionBJ(udg_location02,udg_real05,340.),bj_UNIT_FACING)
	call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1,udg_integer26,GetOwningPlayer(udg_unit03),PolarProjectionBJ(udg_location02,udg_real05,360.),bj_UNIT_FACING)
	call ForGroupBJ(GetUnitsOfTypeIdAll(udg_integer26),function Trig_CF_Cast_Func028A)
	call EnableTrigger(udg_trigger02)
endfunction

function Trig_CF_Loop_Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
	return(udg_integer25==3)
endfunction

function Trig_CF_Loop_Func003Func001Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
	return((IsUnitType(GetEnumUnit(),UNIT_TYPE_STRUCTURE)==false)and(IsUnitAliveBJ(GetEnumUnit()))and(IsUnitEnemy(GetEnumUnit(),GetOwningPlayer(udg_unit03)))and(GetEnumUnit()!=udg_unit03))!=null
endfunction

function Trig_CF_Loop_Func003Func001A takes nothing returns nothing
	if(Trig_CF_Loop_Func003Func001Func001C())then
		call AddSpecialEffectLocBJ(GetUnitLoc(GetEnumUnit()),"Abilities\\Spells\\Items\\AIfb\\AIfbSpecialArt.mdl")
		call UnitDamageTargetBJ(udg_unit03,GetEnumUnit(),udg_real04,ATTACK_TYPE_MAGIC,DAMAGE_TYPE_NORMAL)
	endif
endfunction

function Trig_CF_Loop_Func003C takes nothing returns boolean
	return(udg_integer25!=0)
endfunction

function Trig_CF_Loop_Func004C takes nothing returns boolean
	return(udg_integer25==0)
endfunction

function Trig_CF_Loop_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
	set udg_integer25=(udg_integer25-1)
	if(Trig_CF_Loop_Func002C())then
		call DestroyEffect(udg_effect01)
	endif
	if(Trig_CF_Loop_Func003C())then
		call ForGroupBJ(GetUnitsInRangeOfLocAll(udg_real05,udg_location02),function Trig_CF_Loop_Func003Func001A)
	endif
	if(Trig_CF_Loop_Func004C())then
		call DisableTrigger(GetTriggeringTrigger())
	endif
endfunction

function Trig_Stampede_Cast_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
	return(GetSpellAbilityId()=='A04Y')
endfunction

function Trig_Stampede_Cast_Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
	return(udg_boolean02)
endfunction

function Trig_Stampede_Cast_Func002Func002002 takes nothing returns nothing
	call GroupRemoveUnit(udg_group01,GetEnumUnit())
endfunction

function Trig_Stampede_Cast_Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
	return(udg_boolean02==false)
endfunction

function Trig_Stampede_Cast_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
	if(Trig_Stampede_Cast_Func001C())then
		call DisplayTextToForce(GetForceOfPlayer(GetOwningPlayer(GetSpellAbilityUnit())),(udg_strings01[$A]+"Someone already casted this ability, try again after few seconds."))
	endif
	if(Trig_Stampede_Cast_Func002C())then
		call PlaySoundBJ(udg_sound17)
		call ForGroupBJ(GetUnitsInRectAll(bj_mapInitialPlayableArea),function Trig_Stampede_Cast_Func002Func002002)
		set udg_unit01=GetSpellAbilityUnit()
		set udg_real01=AngleBetweenPoints(GetUnitLoc(udg_unit01),GetSpellTargetLoc())
		set udg_real02=200.
		set udg_real03=150.
		set udg_integer15=0
		set udg_boolean02=true
		call SetUnitInvulnerable(udg_unit01,true)
		call PauseUnit(udg_unit01,true)
		call SetUnitPathing(udg_unit01,false)
		call EnableTrigger(udg_trigger04)
	endif
endfunction

function Trig_Stampede_Loop_Func002Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
	return(IsTerrainPathableBJ(GetUnitLoc(udg_unit01),PATHING_TYPE_WALKABILITY)==false)
endfunction

function Trig_Stampede_Loop_Func002Func003Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
	return((IsUnitInGroup(udg_unit02,udg_group01)==false)and(IsUnitEnemy(udg_unit02,GetOwningPlayer(udg_unit01)))and(IsUnitType(udg_unit02,UNIT_TYPE_STRUCTURE)==false)and(IsUnitAliveBJ(udg_unit02)))!=null
endfunction

function Trig_Stampede_Loop_Func002Func003A takes nothing returns nothing
	set udg_unit02=GetEnumUnit()
	if(Trig_Stampede_Loop_Func002Func003Func002C())then
		call UnitDamageTargetBJ(udg_unit01,udg_unit02,udg_real02,ATTACK_TYPE_NORMAL,DAMAGE_TYPE_NORMAL)
		call GroupAddUnit(udg_group01,udg_unit02)
	endif
endfunction

function Trig_Stampede_Loop_Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
	return(udg_integer15!=40)
endfunction

function Trig_Stampede_Loop_Func003Func006Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
	return((IsUnitEnemy(udg_unit02,GetOwningPlayer(udg_unit01)))and(IsUnitType(udg_unit02,UNIT_TYPE_STRUCTURE)==false)and(IsUnitAliveBJ(udg_unit02)))!=null
endfunction

function Trig_Stampede_Loop_Func003Func006A takes nothing returns nothing
	set udg_unit02=GetEnumUnit()
	if(Trig_Stampede_Loop_Func003Func006Func002C())then
		call UnitDamageTargetBJ(udg_unit01,udg_unit02,udg_real02,ATTACK_TYPE_NORMAL,DAMAGE_TYPE_NORMAL)
	endif
endfunction

function Trig_Stampede_Loop_Func003C takes nothing returns boolean
	return(udg_integer15==40)
endfunction

function Trig_Stampede_Loop_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
	set udg_integer15=(udg_integer15+1)
	if(Trig_Stampede_Loop_Func002C())then
		if(Trig_Stampede_Loop_Func002Func001C())then
			call SetUnitPositionLoc(udg_unit01,PolarProjectionBJ(GetUnitLoc(udg_unit01),25.,udg_real01))
		endif
		call AddSpecialEffectLocBJ(GetUnitLoc(udg_unit01),"Abilities\\Spells\\Items\\AIfb\\AIfbSpecialArt.mdl")
		call ForGroupBJ(GetUnitsInRangeOfLocAll(udg_real03,GetUnitLoc(udg_unit01)),function Trig_Stampede_Loop_Func002Func003A)
	endif
	if(Trig_Stampede_Loop_Func003C())then
		set udg_boolean02=false
		call PauseUnit(udg_unit01,false)
		call SetUnitInvulnerable(udg_unit01,false)
		call SetUnitPathing(udg_unit01,true)
		call AddSpecialEffectLocBJ(GetUnitLoc(udg_unit01),"Abilities\\Spells\\Orc\\WarStomp\\WarStompCaster.mdl")
		call ForGroupBJ(GetUnitsInRangeOfLocAll((udg_real03*2.),GetUnitLoc(udg_unit01)),function Trig_Stampede_Loop_Func003Func006A)
		call DisableTrigger(GetTriggeringTrigger())
	endif
endfunction

function Trig_Tips_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
	call DisplayTextToForce(bj_FORCE_ALL_PLAYERS,(udg_strings01[$A]+"[Tip] Para ganar la partida debes destruir todos los Zombie Towers."))
	call TriggerSleepAction(60.)
	call DisplayTextToForce(bj_FORCE_ALL_PLAYERS,(udg_strings01[$A]+"[Tip] Ganaras oro mantando zombies y animales."))
	call TriggerSleepAction(60.)
	call DisplayTextToForce(bj_FORCE_ALL_PLAYERS,(udg_strings01[$A]+"[Tip] Si quieres mejorar a tu heroe tipea -H."))
	call TriggerSleepAction(60.)
	call DisplayTextToForce(bj_FORCE_ALL_PLAYERS,(udg_strings01[$A]+"[Tip] Si quieres todos los comandos de quest, tipea -qcmds."))
	call TriggerSleepAction(60.)
	call DisplayTextToForce(bj_FORCE_ALL_PLAYERS,(udg_strings01[$A]+"[Tip] Cada 10 minutos aparecer√° un boss en el mapa, Hay un total de 9 bosses."))
	call TriggerSleepAction(60.)
	call DisplayTextToForce(bj_FORCE_ALL_PLAYERS,(udg_strings01[$A]+"[Tip] Al tipear -Q, es probable que no aparesca texto verde. Mala suerte, cancela el quest, reintentalo."))
	call TriggerSleepAction(60.)
	call DisplayTextToForce(bj_FORCE_ALL_PLAYERS,(udg_strings01[$A]+"[Tip] El primero que muere es gay."))
endfunction

	endif
	if(Trig_move_item_Func002C())then

	endif

		call UnitAddItem(udg_units03[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))],UnitItemInSlotBJ(udg_units01[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))],4))
		call DisplayTextToForce(GetForceOfPlayer(GetTriggerPlayer()),(udg_strings01[$A]+"You succesfully moved your item to chest.|r"))
	endif
	if(Trig_move_item_Func005C())then
		call UnitAddItem(udg_units03[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))],UnitItemInSlotBJ(udg_units01[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))],5))
		call DisplayTextToForce(GetForceOfPlayer(GetTriggerPlayer()),(udg_strings01[$A]+"You succesfully moved your item to chest.|r"))
	endif
	if(Trig_move_item_Func006C())then

		call DisplayTextToForce(GetForceOfPlayer(GetTriggerPlayer()),(udg_strings01[$A]+"You succesfully moved your item to chest.|r"))
	endif
	if(Trig_move_item_Func007C())then
		call UnitAddItem(udg_units03[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))],UnitItemInSlotBJ(udg_units01[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))],1))

function Trig_dropp_pick_items_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
	if(Trig_dropp_pick_items_Func001C())then
		call UnitRemoveItemSwapped(UnitItemInSlotBJ(udg_units03[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))],1),udg_units03[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))])
		call DisplayTextToForce(GetForceOfPlayer(GetTriggerPlayer()),(udg_strings01[$A]+"You succesfully dropped your item from chest.|r"))
	endif
	if(Trig_dropp_pick_items_Func002C())then
		call UnitRemoveItemSwapped(UnitItemInSlotBJ(udg_units03[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))],2),udg_units03[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))])
		call DisplayTextToForce(GetForceOfPlayer(GetTriggerPlayer()),(udg_strings01[$A]+"You succesfully dropped your item from chest.|r"))
	endif
	if(Trig_dropp_pick_items_Func003C())then
		call UnitRemoveItemSwapped(UnitItemInSlotBJ(udg_units03[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))],3),udg_units03[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))])
		call DisplayTextToForce(GetForceOfPlayer(GetTriggerPlayer()),(udg_strings01[$A]+"You succesfully dropped your item from chest.|r"))
	endif
	if(Trig_dropp_pick_items_Func004C())then
		call UnitRemoveItemSwapped(UnitItemInSlotBJ(udg_units03[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))],4),udg_units03[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))])
		call DisplayTextToForce(GetForceOfPlayer(GetTriggerPlayer()),(udg_strings01[$A]+"You succesfully dropped your item from chest.|r"))
	endif
	if(Trig_dropp_pick_items_Func005C())then
		call UnitRemoveItemSwapped(UnitItemInSlotBJ(udg_units03[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))],5),udg_units03[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))])
		call DisplayTextToForce(GetForceOfPlayer(GetTriggerPlayer()),(udg_strings01[$A]+"You succesfully dropped your item from chest.|r"))
	endif
	if(Trig_dropp_pick_items_Func006C())then
		call UnitRemoveItemSwapped(UnitItemInSlotBJ(udg_units03[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))],6),udg_units03[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))])
		call DisplayTextToForce(GetForceOfPlayer(GetTriggerPlayer()),(udg_strings01[$A]+"You succesfully dropped your item from chest.|r"))
	endif
	if(Trig_dropp_pick_items_Func007C())then
		call UnitRemoveItemSwapped(UnitItemInSlotBJ(udg_units03[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))],1),udg_units03[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))])
		call UnitRemoveItemSwapped(UnitItemInSlotBJ(udg_units03[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))],2),udg_units03[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))])
		call UnitRemoveItemSwapped(UnitItemInSlotBJ(udg_units03[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))],3),udg_units03[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))])
		call UnitRemoveItemSwapped(UnitItemInSlotBJ(udg_units03[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))],4),udg_units03[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))])
		call UnitRemoveItemSwapped(UnitItemInSlotBJ(udg_units03[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))],5),udg_units03[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))])
		call UnitRemoveItemSwapped(UnitItemInSlotBJ(udg_units03[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))],6),udg_units03[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))])

		call DisplayTextToForce(GetForceOfPlayer(GetTriggerPlayer()),(udg_strings01[$A]+"You succesfully picked your items near chest.|r"))
		call EnumItemsInRectBJ(RectFromCenterSizeBJ(GetUnitLoc(udg_units03[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))]),250.,250.),function Trig_dropp_pick_items_Func008Func002A)
	endif
endfunction

	return(udg_integer13==1)
endfunction

function Trig_hero_kill_sansa_carte_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
	set udg_integer13=GetRandomInt(1,5)
	if(Trig_hero_kill_sansa_carte_Func002C())then
		set udg_integer14=GetRandomInt(1,5)
		if(Trig_hero_kill_sansa_carte_Func002Func002001())then
			call CreateItemLoc('I031',GetUnitLoc(GetDyingUnit()))
		endif
		if(Trig_hero_kill_sansa_carte_Func002Func003001())then
			call CreateItemLoc('I02X',GetUnitLoc(GetDyingUnit()))
		endif
		if(Trig_hero_kill_sansa_carte_Func002Func004001())then
			call CreateItemLoc('I02Y',GetUnitLoc(GetDyingUnit()))
		endif
		if(Trig_hero_kill_sansa_carte_Func002Func005001())then
			call CreateItemLoc('I02Z',GetUnitLoc(GetDyingUnit()))
		endif
		if(Trig_hero_kill_sansa_carte_Func002Func006001())then
			call CreateItemLoc('I030',GetUnitLoc(GetDyingUnit()))
		endif
		if(Trig_hero_kill_sansa_carte_Func002Func007001())then
			call CreateItemLoc('I033',GetUnitLoc(GetDyingUnit()))
		endif	
	endif
	set udg_integer13=GetRandomInt(1,1)
	if(Trig_hero_kill_sansa_carte_Func002C())then
		set udg_integer14=GetRandomInt(6,10)	
		if(Trig_hero_kill_sansa_carte_Func002Func008001())then
			call CreateItemLoc('rspl',GetUnitLoc(GetDyingUnit()))
		endif
		if(Trig_hero_kill_sansa_carte_Func002Func009001())then
			call CreateItemLoc('rma2',GetUnitLoc(GetDyingUnit()))
		endif
		if(Trig_hero_kill_sansa_carte_Func002Func010001())then
			call CreateItemLoc('rhe3',GetUnitLoc(GetDyingUnit()))
		endif
		if(Trig_hero_kill_sansa_carte_Func002Func011001())then
			call CreateItemLoc('rsps',GetUnitLoc(GetDyingUnit()))
		endif
		if(Trig_hero_kill_sansa_carte_Func002Func011001())then
			call CreateItemLoc('rspd',GetUnitLoc(GetDyingUnit()))
		endif
	endif		
endfunction

function Trig_animal_dies_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean

function Trig_animal_dies_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
	set udg_integer08=GetRandomInt(1,$F)
	call CreateTextTagUnitBJ((udg_strings01[(1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetKillingUnit())))]+("+"+I2S(udg_integer08))),GetDyingUnit(),0,$A,'d','d','d',0)
	call SetTextTagPermanentBJ(bj_lastCreatedTextTag,false)
	call SetTextTagLifespanBJ(bj_lastCreatedTextTag,4.)
	call SetTextTagFadepointBJ(bj_lastCreatedTextTag,1.)
	call SetTextTagVelocityBJ(bj_lastCreatedTextTag,32.,90)
	call AdjustPlayerStateBJ(udg_integer08,GetOwningPlayer(GetKillingUnit()),PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_GOLD)
	call AddHeroXPSwapped((udg_integer08*3),GetKillingUnit(),true)
	call TriggerSleepAction(10.)
	call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1,'n008',Player($F),GetRandomLocInRect(udg_rect08),bj_UNIT_FACING)
endfunction

function Trig_healing_salve_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
	return(GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit())=='h00S')and(UnitHasItemOfTypeBJ(GetTriggerUnit(),'I010'))and(UnitHasItemOfTypeBJ(GetTriggerUnit(),'I00V'))
endfunction

function Trig_healing_salve_Func007Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
	return(udg_integers09[(1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit())))]==1)
endfunction

function Trig_healing_salve_Func007C takes nothing returns boolean
	return(udg_integers07[(1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit())))]==2)
endfunction

function Trig_healing_salve_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
	call RemoveItem(GetItemOfTypeFromUnitBJ(GetTriggerUnit(),'I010'))
	call RemoveItem(GetItemOfTypeFromUnitBJ(GetTriggerUnit(),'I00V'))
	call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped('I012',GetTriggerUnit())
	call AddSpecialEffectTargetUnitBJ("overhead",GetTriggerUnit(),"Abilities\\Spells\\Items\\AIil\\AIilTarget.mdl")
	if(Trig_healing_salve_Func007C())then
		set udg_integers09[(1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit())))]=(udg_integers09[(1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit())))]+1)
		if(Trig_healing_salve_Func007Func002C())then
			set udg_integer17=GetRandomInt($96,300)
			set udg_integer18=GetRandomInt($96,300)
			set udg_integer24=GetRandomInt(75,$AF)
			call DisplayTextToForce(bj_FORCE_ALL_PLAYERS,(udg_strings01[(1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit())))]+(GetPlayerName(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))+(udg_strings01[7]+(" has succesfully completed a quest and received "+(I2S(udg_integer17)+(" gold, "+(I2S(udg_integer18)+(" lumber and "+(I2S(udg_integer24)+" quest points."))))))))))
			set udg_integers19[(1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit())))]=(udg_integers19[(1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit())))]+udg_integer24)
			set udg_integers07[(1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit())))]=0
			call AdjustPlayerStateBJ(udg_integer17,GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()),PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_GOLD)
			call AdjustPlayerStateBJ(udg_integer18,GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()),PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_LUMBER)
			set udg_integers20[(1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit())))]=(udg_integers20[(1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit())))]+1)
		endif
	endif
endfunction

endfunction

function Trig_cose_gate_Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
	return(CountUnitsInGroup(GetUnitsInRangeOfLocAll(100.,GetUnitLoc(GetSpellAbilityUnit())))>=2)
endfunction

function Trig_cose_gate_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
	if(Trig_cose_gate_Func001C())then
		call ReplaceUnitBJ(GetSpellAbilityUnit(),'h00H',1)
		call SelectUnitForPlayerSingle(bj_lastReplacedUnit,GetOwningPlayer(GetSpellAbilityUnit()))
	endif
	if(Trig_cose_gate_Func002C())then
		call DisplayTextToForce(GetForceOfPlayer(GetOwningPlayer(GetSpellAbilityUnit())),(udg_strings01[$A]+"The gate is blocked!|r"))
	endif
endfunction

function Trig_no_build_in_trees_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
	return(IsUnitType(GetEnteringUnit(),UNIT_TYPE_STRUCTURE))!=null
endfunction

function Trig_no_build_in_trees_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
	call KillUnit(GetEnteringUnit())
	call DisplayTextToForce(GetForceOfPlayer(GetOwningPlayer(GetEnteringUnit())),(udg_strings01[$A]+"You don't have permission to build in forest!|r"))
endfunction

endfunction

function Trig_INITIALIZATION_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
	if(Trig_INITIALIZATION_Func001C())then
		call DisplayTextToForce(bj_FORCE_ALL_PLAYERS,(udg_strings01[$C]+(GetPlayerName(Player($B))+(udg_strings01[$A]+" has been kicked because isn't allowed to play as Zombie!|r"))))
		call CustomDefeatBJ(Player($B),"Isn't allowed to play as Zombie!")
		call SetPlayerName(Player($B),"Zombie")
	endif
	set udg_integer12=$A
	set udg_booleans01[$C]=true
	call EnumDestructablesInRectAll(udg_rect08,function Trig_INITIALIZATION_Func004002)
	call SetDestructableInvulnerable(udg_destructable06,true)
	call SetDestructableInvulnerable(udg_destructable04,true)
	call SetDestructableInvulnerable(udg_destructable03,true)
	call SetDestructableInvulnerable(udg_destructable05,true)
	set udg_booleans04[1]=false
	set udg_booleans04[2]=false
	set udg_booleans04[3]=false
	set udg_booleans04[4]=false
	set udg_booleans04[5]=false
	set udg_booleans04[6]=false
	set udg_booleans04[7]=false
	set udg_booleans04[8]=false
	set udg_booleans04[9]=false
	set udg_booleans04[$A]=false
	set udg_booleans01[$B]=true
	set udg_integer01=$A
	set udg_strings01[1]="|cffff0000"
	set udg_strings01[2]="|cff0000ff"
	set udg_strings01[3]="|cff00ffff"
	set udg_strings01[4]="|cff8000ff"
	set udg_strings01[5]="|cffffff00"
	set udg_strings01[6]="|cffff8000"
	set udg_strings01[7]="|cff00ff00"
	set udg_strings01[8]="|cffff00ff"
	set udg_strings01[9]="|cff808080"
	set udg_strings01[$A]="|cff8C98ff"
	set udg_strings01[$B]="|cff045b00"
	set udg_strings01[$C]="|cff804000"
	call CreateMultiboardBJ($A,16,(udg_strings01[udg_integer01]+"Zombie Attack - Statistics|r"))
	set udg_multiboard01=bj_lastCreatedMultiboard
	call MultiboardSetItemStyleBJ(udg_multiboard01,1,bj_forLoopAIndex,true,false)
	call MultiboardSetItemStyleBJ(udg_multiboard01,2,bj_forLoopAIndex,true,false)
	call MultiboardSetItemStyleBJ(udg_multiboard01,3,bj_forLoopAIndex,true,false)
	call MultiboardSetItemStyleBJ(udg_multiboard01,4,bj_forLoopAIndex,true,false)
	call MultiboardSetItemStyleBJ(udg_multiboard01,5,bj_forLoopAIndex,true,false)
	call MultiboardSetItemStyleBJ(udg_multiboard01,6,bj_forLoopAIndex,true,false)
	call MultiboardSetItemStyleBJ(udg_multiboard01,7,bj_forLoopAIndex,true,false)
	call MultiboardSetItemStyleBJ(udg_multiboard01,8,bj_forLoopAIndex,true,false)
	call MultiboardSetItemStyleBJ(udg_multiboard01,9,bj_forLoopAIndex,true,false)
	call MultiboardSetItemStyleBJ(udg_multiboard01,$A,bj_forLoopAIndex,true,false)
	call MultiboardSetItemWidthBJ(udg_multiboard01,1,bj_forLoopAIndex,15.)
	call MultiboardSetItemWidthBJ(udg_multiboard01,2,bj_forLoopAIndex,4.)
	call MultiboardSetItemWidthBJ(udg_multiboard01,3,bj_forLoopAIndex,4.)
	call MultiboardSetItemWidthBJ(udg_multiboard01,4,bj_forLoopAIndex,4.)
	call MultiboardSetItemWidthBJ(udg_multiboard01,5,bj_forLoopAIndex,4.)
	call MultiboardSetItemWidthBJ(udg_multiboard01,6,bj_forLoopAIndex,4.)
	call MultiboardSetItemWidthBJ(udg_multiboard01,8,bj_forLoopAIndex,4.)
	call MultiboardSetItemWidthBJ(udg_multiboard01,9,bj_forLoopAIndex,6.)
	call MultiboardSetItemWidthBJ(udg_multiboard01,$A,bj_forLoopAIndex,4.)
	call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_multiboard01,1,1,(udg_strings01[udg_integer01]+"Player Name|r"))
	call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_multiboard01,2,1,(udg_strings01[udg_integer01]+"Kills|r"))
	call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_multiboard01,3,1,(udg_strings01[udg_integer01]+"Deaths|r"))
	call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_multiboard01,4,1,(udg_strings01[udg_integer01]+"Gold|r"))

	call EnableTrigger(udg_trigger74)

	call TriggerExecute(udg_trigger204)
	call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_multiboard01,2,$D,(udg_strings01[udg_integer01]+"Easy|r"))
	call SetPlayerHandicapBJ(Player($B),25.)
	if(Trig_No_difficulty_selected_Func009001())then
		call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1,'e000',Player(0),GetUnitLoc(udg_unit05),bj_UNIT_FACING)
	endif
	if(Trig_No_difficulty_selected_Func010001())then
		call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1,'e000',Player(1),GetUnitLoc(udg_unit05),bj_UNIT_FACING)
	endif
	if(Trig_No_difficulty_selected_Func011001())then
		call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1,'e000',Player(2),GetUnitLoc(udg_unit05),bj_UNIT_FACING)
	endif
	if(Trig_No_difficulty_selected_Func012001())then
		call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1,'e000',Player(3),GetUnitLoc(udg_unit05),bj_UNIT_FACING)
	endif
	if(Trig_No_difficulty_selected_Func013001())then
		call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1,'e000',Player(4),GetUnitLoc(udg_unit05),bj_UNIT_FACING)
	endif
	if(Trig_No_difficulty_selected_Func014001())then
		call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1,'e000',Player(5),GetUnitLoc(udg_unit05),bj_UNIT_FACING)
	endif
	if(Trig_No_difficulty_selected_Func015001())then
		call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1,'e000',Player(6),GetUnitLoc(udg_unit05),bj_UNIT_FACING)
	endif
	if(Trig_No_difficulty_selected_Func016001())then
		call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1,'e000',Player(7),GetUnitLoc(udg_unit05),bj_UNIT_FACING)
	endif
	if(Trig_No_difficulty_selected_Func017001())then
		call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1,'e000',Player(8),GetUnitLoc(udg_unit05),bj_UNIT_FACING)

	if(Trig_No_difficulty_selected_Func018001())then

	return(GetUnitTypeId(GetEnteringUnit())=='h01B')

function Trig_gold_mine_build_Func001Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
	return((IsUnitType(GetEnumUnit(),UNIT_TYPE_STRUCTURE))and(GetOwningPlayer(GetEnumUnit())==GetOwningPlayer(GetEnteringUnit()))and(GetUnitTypeId(GetEnumUnit())=='h000'))!=null
endfunction

function Trig_gold_mine_build_Func001A takes nothing returns nothing
	if(Trig_gold_mine_build_Func001Func001C())then
		call DisplayTextToForce(GetForceOfPlayer(GetOwningPlayer(GetEnteringUnit())),(udg_strings01[$A]+"You don't have permission to build Gold Mine near (400 range) your Tent!|r"))
		call KillUnit(GetEnteringUnit())
		call AdjustPlayerStateBJ(500,GetOwningPlayer(GetEnteringUnit()),PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_LUMBER)
	endif
endfunction

function Trig_gold_mine_build_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
	call ForGroupBJ(GetUnitsInRangeOfLocAll(400.,GetUnitLoc(GetEnteringUnit())),function Trig_gold_mine_build_Func001A)
endfunction

function Trig_Hero_Sold_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
	return(IsUnitType(GetSoldUnit(),UNIT_TYPE_HERO))!=null
endfunction

function Trig_Hero_Sold_Func020002 takes nothing returns nothing
	call SetPlayerTechMaxAllowedSwap(GetUnitTypeId(GetSoldUnit()),0,GetEnumPlayer())
endfunction

function Trig_Hero_Sold_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
	set udg_booleans01[(1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetBuyingUnit())))]=true
	call DisplayTextToForce(bj_FORCE_ALL_PLAYERS,(udg_strings01[(1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetBuyingUnit())))]+(GetPlayerName(GetOwningPlayer(GetBuyingUnit()))+(udg_strings01[$A]+(" has chosen|r "+(GetUnitName(GetSoldUnit())+(udg_strings01[$A]+".|r")))))))
	call RemoveUnit(GetBuyingUnit())
	call PanCameraToTimedLocForPlayer(GetOwningPlayer(GetBuyingUnit()),GetPlayerStartLocationLoc(GetOwningPlayer(GetBuyingUnit())),0)
	call SetPlayerMaxHeroesAllowed(0,GetOwningPlayer(GetBuyingUnit()))
	call SetUnitPositionLoc(GetSoldUnit(),GetPlayerStartLocationLoc(GetOwningPlayer(GetBuyingUnit())))
	set udg_units01[(1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetBuyingUnit())))]=GetSoldUnit()
	call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1,'n000',GetOwningPlayer(GetBuyingUnit()),GetPlayerStartLocationLoc(GetOwningPlayer(GetBuyingUnit())),bj_UNIT_FACING)
	set udg_units02[(1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetBuyingUnit())))]=bj_lastCreatedUnit
	call ClearSelectionForPlayer(GetOwningPlayer(GetBuyingUnit()))
	call SelectUnitAddForPlayer(udg_units01[(1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetBuyingUnit())))],GetOwningPlayer(GetBuyingUnit()))
	call SelectUnitAddForPlayer(udg_units02[(1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetBuyingUnit())))],GetOwningPlayer(GetBuyingUnit()))
	call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_multiboard01,1,((1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetBuyingUnit())))+1),(udg_strings01[(1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetBuyingUnit())))]+(GetPlayerName(GetOwningPlayer(GetBuyingUnit()))+(udg_strings01[7]+" [Alive]|r"))))
	call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_multiboard01,2,((1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetBuyingUnit())))+1),(udg_strings01[udg_integer01]+"0|r"))
	call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_multiboard01,3,((1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetBuyingUnit())))+1),(udg_strings01[udg_integer01]+"0|r"))
	call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_multiboard01,4,((1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetBuyingUnit())))+1),(udg_strings01[udg_integer01]+"0|r"))
	call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_multiboard01,5,((1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetBuyingUnit())))+1),(udg_strings01[udg_integer01]+"0|r"))
	call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_multiboard01,6,((1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetBuyingUnit())))+1),(udg_strings01[udg_integer01]+"100%|r"))
	call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_multiboard01,7,((1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetBuyingUnit())))+1),(udg_strings01[udg_integer01]+"100%|r"))
	call ForForce(bj_FORCE_ALL_PLAYERS,function Trig_Hero_Sold_Func020002)
endfunction

function Trig_every_seconds_Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
	return(udg_integer02==60)
endfunction

function Trig_every_seconds_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
	set udg_integer02=(udg_integer02+1)
	if(Trig_every_seconds_Func002C())then
		set udg_integer02=0
		set udg_integer03=(udg_integer03+1)
		call SetPlayerTechResearchedSwap('R00E',(GetPlayerTechCountSimple('R00E',Player($B))+1),Player($B))
	endif
	call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_multiboard01,2,$F,(udg_strings01[udg_integer01]+(I2S(udg_integer03)+(":"+I2S(udg_integer02)))))
endfunction

function Trig_Clicked_easy_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
	call EnableTrigger(udg_trigger74)
	set udg_boolean01=true
	call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_multiboard01,2,$D,(udg_strings01[udg_integer01]+"Easy|r"))
	call DisplayTextToForce(bj_FORCE_ALL_PLAYERS,(udg_strings01[1]+(GetPlayerName(Player(0))+(udg_strings01[$A]+(" has selected difficulty|r easy"+(udg_strings01[$A]+".|r"))))))
	call TriggerExecute(udg_trigger187)
	call TriggerExecute(udg_trigger204)
	call SetPlayerHandicapBJ(Player($B),25.)
	if(Trig_Clicked_easy_Func008001())then
		call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1,'e000',Player(0),GetUnitLoc(udg_unit05),bj_UNIT_FACING)
	endif
	if(Trig_Clicked_easy_Func009001())then
		call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1,'e000',Player(1),GetUnitLoc(udg_unit05),bj_UNIT_FACING)
	endif
	if(Trig_Clicked_easy_Func010001())then
		call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1,'e000',Player(2),GetUnitLoc(udg_unit05),bj_UNIT_FACING)
	endif
	if(Trig_Clicked_easy_Func011001())then
		call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1,'e000',Player(3),GetUnitLoc(udg_unit05),bj_UNIT_FACING)
	endif
	if(Trig_Clicked_easy_Func012001())then
		call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1,'e000',Player(4),GetUnitLoc(udg_unit05),bj_UNIT_FACING)
	endif
	if(Trig_Clicked_easy_Func013001())then
		call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1,'e000',Player(5),GetUnitLoc(udg_unit05),bj_UNIT_FACING)
	endif
	if(Trig_Clicked_easy_Func014001())then
		call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1,'e000',Player(6),GetUnitLoc(udg_unit05),bj_UNIT_FACING)
	endif
	if(Trig_Clicked_easy_Func015001())then
		call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1,'e000',Player(7),GetUnitLoc(udg_unit05),bj_UNIT_FACING)
	endif
	if(Trig_Clicked_easy_Func016001())then
		call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1,'e000',Player(8),GetUnitLoc(udg_unit05),bj_UNIT_FACING)
	endif
	if(Trig_Clicked_easy_Func017001())then
		call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1,'e000',Player(9),GetUnitLoc(udg_unit05),bj_UNIT_FACING)
	endif
	call CreateTimerDialogBJ(udg_timer01,"|cff8C98ffTime remaining . . .|r")
	set udg_timerdialog01=bj_lastCreatedTimerDialog
	call StartTimerBJ(udg_timer01,false,600.)
endfunction

function Trig_Anti_Ally_Kills_Func004C takes nothing returns boolean
	return(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit())==Player(0))or(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit())==Player(1))or(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit())==Player(2))or(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit())==Player(3))or(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit())==Player(4))or(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit())==Player(5))or(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit())==Player(6))or(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit())==Player(7))or(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit())==Player(8))or(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit())==Player(9))

function Trig_Anti_Ally_Kills_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean

	endif
endfunction

function Trig_player_leaves_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
	if(Trig_player_leaves_Func001C())then
		call DialogDisplayBJ(false,udg_dialog02,GetTriggerPlayer())
		set udg_boolean03=false
		set udg_booleans03[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))]=false
	endif
	call ForceRemovePlayer(udg_force01,GetTriggerPlayer())
	call DisplayTextToForce(bj_FORCE_ALL_PLAYERS,(udg_strings01[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))]+(GetPlayerName(GetTriggerPlayer())+(udg_strings01[$A]+" has left the game."))))
	call DisplayTextToForce(bj_FORCE_ALL_PLAYERS,(udg_strings01[$A]+"All his units and structures were removed."))
	call ForGroupBJ(GetUnitsOfPlayerAll(GetTriggerPlayer()),function Trig_player_leaves_Func005002)
	call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_multiboard01,1,((1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))+1),(udg_strings01[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))]+(GetPlayerName(GetTriggerPlayer())+(udg_strings01[9]+(" [Left at "+(I2S(udg_integer03)+(":"+(I2S(udg_integer02)+"]"))))))))
	call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_multiboard01,2,((1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))+1),(udg_strings01[udg_integer01]+"-|r"))
	call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_multiboard01,3,((1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))+1),(udg_strings01[udg_integer01]+"-|r"))
	call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_multiboard01,4,((1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))+1),(udg_strings01[udg_integer01]+"-|r"))
	call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_multiboard01,5,((1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))+1),(udg_strings01[udg_integer01]+"-|r"))
	call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_multiboard01,6,((1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))+1),(udg_strings01[udg_integer01]+"-|r"))
	call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_multiboard01,7,((1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))+1),(udg_strings01[udg_integer01]+"-|r"))
	call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_multiboard01,8,((1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))+1),(udg_strings01[udg_integer01]+"-|r"))

	call SetPlayerTechMaxAllowedSwap('h01G',1,GetOwningPlayer(GetDyingUnit()))
	call SetPlayerTechMaxAllowedSwap('h01H',1,GetOwningPlayer(GetDyingUnit()))
	call SetPlayerTechMaxAllowedSwap('h01I',1,GetOwningPlayer(GetDyingUnit()))
	call ForceRemovePlayer(udg_force01,GetOwningPlayer(GetDyingUnit()))
	call PlaySoundBJ(udg_sound05)
	call ForGroupBJ(GetUnitsOfPlayerAll(GetOwningPlayer(GetDyingUnit())),function Trig_hero_dies_Func008002)
	call DisplayTextToForce(bj_FORCE_ALL_PLAYERS,(udg_strings01[(1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetDyingUnit())))]+(GetPlayerName(GetOwningPlayer(GetDyingUnit()))+(udg_strings01[$A]+(" fue asesinado por a|r "+(GetUnitName(GetKillingUnit())+(udg_strings01[$A]+"!!|r")))))))
	call DisplayTextToForce(bj_FORCE_ALL_PLAYERS,(udg_strings01[$A]+"La base de la victima fue destruida. Este jugador revivir√° en 1 minuto."))
	call DisplayTimedTextToForce(GetForceOfPlayer(GetOwningPlayer(GetDyingUnit())),60.,(udg_strings01[$A]+("Haras respawn en|r "+(I2S((udg_integer03+5))+(":"+(I2S(udg_integer02)+(udg_strings01[$A]+".")))))))
	call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_multiboard01,1,((1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetDyingUnit())))+1),(udg_strings01[(1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetDyingUnit())))]+(GetPlayerName(GetOwningPlayer(GetDyingUnit()))+(udg_strings01[1]+(" [Dead at "+(I2S(udg_integer03)+(":"+(I2S(udg_integer02)+"]"))))))))
	call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_multiboard01,6,((1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetDyingUnit())))+1),(udg_strings01[udg_integer01]+"-|r"))
	call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_multiboard01,7,((1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetDyingUnit())))+1),(udg_strings01[udg_integer01]+"-|r"))
	call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_multiboard01,8,((1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetDyingUnit())))+1),(udg_strings01[udg_integer01]+"-|r"))
	call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_multiboard01,$A,((1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetDyingUnit())))+1),(udg_strings01[udg_integer01]+"-|r"))
	call TriggerSleepAction(60.)
	if(Trig_hero_dies_Func018C())then
		call ForceAddPlayer(udg_force01,GetOwningPlayer(GetDyingUnit()))
		call DisplayTextToForce(bj_FORCE_ALL_PLAYERS,(udg_strings01[(1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetDyingUnit())))]+(GetPlayerName(GetOwningPlayer(GetDyingUnit()))+(udg_strings01[$A]+" has been respawned.|r"))))
		call PanCameraToTimedLocForPlayer(GetOwningPlayer(GetDyingUnit()),GetPlayerStartLocationLoc(GetOwningPlayer(GetDyingUnit())),0)
		call ReviveHeroLoc(GetDyingUnit(),GetPlayerStartLocationLoc(GetOwningPlayer(GetDyingUnit())),true)
		call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1,'n000',GetOwningPlayer(GetDyingUnit()),GetPlayerStartLocationLoc(GetOwningPlayer(GetDyingUnit())),bj_UNIT_FACING)
		set udg_units02[(1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetDyingUnit())))]=bj_lastCreatedUnit
		call ClearSelectionForPlayer(GetOwningPlayer(GetDyingUnit()))
		call SelectUnitAddForPlayer(udg_units01[(1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetDyingUnit())))],GetOwningPlayer(GetDyingUnit()))
		call SelectUnitAddForPlayer(udg_units02[(1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetDyingUnit())))],GetOwningPlayer(GetDyingUnit()))
		call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_multiboard01,1,((1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetDyingUnit())))+1),(udg_strings01[(1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetDyingUnit())))]+(GetPlayerName(GetOwningPlayer(GetDyingUnit()))+(udg_strings01[7]+" [Alive]|r"))))
		call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_multiboard01,$A,((1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetDyingUnit())))+1),(udg_strings01[udg_integer01]+"0/25|r"))
	endif

	set udg_integer12=(udg_integer12-1)
	call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_multiboard01,2,16,(udg_strings01[udg_integer01]+(I2S(udg_integer12)+"|r")))
	set udg_integer10=GetRandomInt($FA,500)

	set udg_integer06=GetRandomInt(1,6)

	if(Trig_statue_dies_WIN_Func010001())then
		call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(udg_integer11,'z000',Player($B),GetUnitLoc(GetDyingUnit()),bj_UNIT_FACING)

	endif
	if(Trig_statue_dies_WIN_Func013001())then

	if(Trig_statue_dies_WIN_Func015001())then

	endif
	if(Trig_statue_dies_WIN_Func021001())then

		call DisableTrigger(udg_trigger77)
		call DisableTrigger(udg_trigger78)
		call DisableTrigger(udg_trigger79)
		call DisableTrigger(udg_trigger72)
		call ForGroupBJ(GetUnitsInRectAll(bj_mapInitialPlayableArea),function Trig_statue_dies_WIN_Func022Func012002)

		call FogMaskEnableOff()

function Trig_build_prima_data_langa_flag_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
	return(GetUnitTypeId(GetEnteringUnit())=='h01A')
endfunction

function Trig_build_prima_data_langa_flag_Func001Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
	return((IsUnitType(GetEnumUnit(),UNIT_TYPE_STRUCTURE))and(GetOwningPlayer(GetEnumUnit())!=GetOwningPlayer(GetEnteringUnit()))and(GetUnitTypeId(GetEnumUnit())=='h01A'))!=null
endfunction

function Trig_build_prima_data_langa_flag_Func001A takes nothing returns nothing
	if(Trig_build_prima_data_langa_flag_Func001Func001C())then
		call DisplayTextToForce(GetForceOfPlayer(GetOwningPlayer(GetEnteringUnit())),(udg_strings01[$A]+("You don't have permission to build a flag near "+(udg_strings01[(1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetEnumUnit())))]+(GetPlayerName(GetOwningPlayer(GetEnumUnit()))+(udg_strings01[$A]+"'s territory!|r"))))))
		call KillUnit(GetEnteringUnit())
	endif
endfunction

function Trig_build_prima_data_langa_flag_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
	call ForGroupBJ(GetUnitsInRangeOfLocAll(1400.,GetUnitLoc(GetEnteringUnit())),function Trig_build_prima_data_langa_flag_Func001A)
endfunction

	return(GetUnitTypeId(GetEnteringUnit())=='h01A')

endfunction

		call KillUnit(GetEnteringUnit())
	endif
endfunction

function Trig_Quest_System_Message_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
	call EnableTrigger(udg_trigger190)
	call EnableTrigger(udg_trigger191)
	call EnableTrigger(udg_trigger192)
	call EnableTrigger(udg_trigger189)
	call DisplayTextToForce(bj_FORCE_ALL_PLAYERS,(udg_strings01[7]+"[Quest System] If you want to see quest commands type -qcmds."))
	call TriggerSleepAction(30.)
	call DisplayTextToForce(bj_FORCE_ALL_PLAYERS,(udg_strings01[7]+"[Quest System] If you want to see quest commands type -qcmds."))
endfunction

function Trig_Qcmds_Actions takes nothing returns nothing

	endif

function Trig_Quest_Command_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
	if(Trig_Quest_Command_Func001001())then
		call DisplayTextToForce(GetForceOfPlayer(GetTriggerPlayer()),(udg_strings01[7]+"You must wait 3 minutes to get a new quest because you canceled a quest."))
	endif
	if(Trig_Quest_Command_Func002001())then
		call DisplayTextToForce(GetForceOfPlayer(GetTriggerPlayer()),(udg_strings01[7]+"You already have a quest!|r"))
	endif
	if(Trig_Quest_Command_Func003001())then
		call DisplayTextToForce(GetForceOfPlayer(GetTriggerPlayer()),(udg_strings01[7]+"Your hero is dead or you don't have a hero.|r"))
	endif
	if(Trig_Quest_Command_Func004C())then
		set udg_integer16=GetRandomInt(1,$C)
		set udg_integers07[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))]=udg_integer16
		if(Trig_Quest_Command_Func004Func003C())then
			call DisplayTextToForce(GetForceOfPlayer(GetTriggerPlayer()),(udg_strings01[7]+"You got a quest: kill 15 animals.|r"))
			set udg_integers08[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))]=0
		endif
		if(Trig_Quest_Command_Func004Func004C())then
			call DisplayTextToForce(GetForceOfPlayer(GetTriggerPlayer()),(udg_strings01[7]+"You got a quest: make 1 potion.|r"))
			set udg_integers09[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))]=0
		endif
		if(Trig_Quest_Command_Func004Func005C())then
			call DisplayTextToForce(GetForceOfPlayer(GetTriggerPlayer()),(udg_strings01[7]+"You got a quest: kill 50 zombies.|r"))
			set udg_integers10[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))]=0
		endif
		if(Trig_Quest_Command_Func004Func006C())then
			call DisplayTextToForce(GetForceOfPlayer(GetTriggerPlayer()),(udg_strings01[7]+"You got the hardest quest: destroy a zombie tower (many extra points).|r"))
			set udg_integers11[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))]=0
		endif
		if(Trig_Quest_Command_Func004Func007C())then
			call DisplayTextToForce(GetForceOfPlayer(GetTriggerPlayer()),(udg_strings01[7]+"You got a quest: cast 12 abilities.|r"))
			set udg_integers12[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))]=0
		endif
		if(Trig_Quest_Command_Func004Func008C())then
			call DisplayTextToForce(GetForceOfPlayer(GetTriggerPlayer()),(udg_strings01[7]+"You got a quest: train 15 units.|r"))
			set udg_integers13[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))]=0
		endif
		if(Trig_Quest_Command_Func004Func009C())then
			call DisplayTextToForce(GetForceOfPlayer(GetTriggerPlayer()),(udg_strings01[7]+"You got a quest: kill 8 frogs.|r"))
			set udg_integers14[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))]=0
		endif
		if(Trig_Quest_Command_Func004Func010C())then
			call DisplayTextToForce(GetForceOfPlayer(GetTriggerPlayer()),(udg_strings01[7]+"You got a quest: kill 8 stags.|r"))
			set udg_integers15[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))]=0
		endif
		if(Trig_Quest_Command_Func004Func011C())then
			call DisplayTextToForce(GetForceOfPlayer(GetTriggerPlayer()),(udg_strings01[7]+"You got a quest: kill 8 raccoons.|r"))
			set udg_integers16[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))]=0
		endif
		if(Trig_Quest_Command_Func004Func012C())then
			call DisplayTextToForce(GetForceOfPlayer(GetTriggerPlayer()),(udg_strings01[7]+"You got a quest: kill 8 rabbits.|r"))
			set udg_integers17[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))]=0
		endif
		if(Trig_Quest_Command_Func004Func013C())then
			call DisplayTextToForce(GetForceOfPlayer(GetTriggerPlayer()),(udg_strings01[7]+"You got a quest: sell 8 items to the shop.|r"))
			set udg_integers18[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))]=0
		endif
	endif
endfunction

function Trig_Myquest_Command_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
	if(Trig_Myquest_Command_Func001001())then
		call DisplayTextToForce(GetForceOfPlayer(GetTriggerPlayer()),(udg_strings01[7]+"Your hero is dead or you don't have a hero.|r"))
	endif
	if(Trig_Myquest_Command_Func002C())then
		if(Trig_Myquest_Command_Func002Func002001())then
			call DisplayTextToForce(GetForceOfPlayer(GetTriggerPlayer()),(udg_strings01[7]+"You don't have a quest! Type -Q to get a quest."))
		endif
		if(Trig_Myquest_Command_Func002Func003001())then
			call DisplayTextToForce(GetForceOfPlayer(GetTriggerPlayer()),(udg_strings01[7]+("Your quest: kill 15 animals. Progress: "+(I2S(udg_integers08[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))])+"/15."))))
		endif
		if(Trig_Myquest_Command_Func002Func004001())then
			call DisplayTextToForce(GetForceOfPlayer(GetTriggerPlayer()),(udg_strings01[7]+("Your quest: make 1 potion. Progress: "+(I2S(udg_integers09[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))])+"/1."))))
		endif
		if(Trig_Myquest_Command_Func002Func005001())then
			call DisplayTextToForce(GetForceOfPlayer(GetTriggerPlayer()),(udg_strings01[7]+("Your quest: kill 50 zombies. Progress: "+(I2S(udg_integers10[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))])+"/50."))))
		endif
		if(Trig_Myquest_Command_Func002Func006001())then
			call DisplayTextToForce(GetForceOfPlayer(GetTriggerPlayer()),(udg_strings01[7]+("Your quest: destroy a zombie tower. Progress: "+(I2S(udg_integers11[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))])+"/1."))))
		endif
		if(Trig_Myquest_Command_Func002Func007001())then
			call DisplayTextToForce(GetForceOfPlayer(GetTriggerPlayer()),(udg_strings01[7]+("Your quest: cast 5 abilities. Progress: "+(I2S(udg_integers12[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))])+"/5."))))
		endif
		if(Trig_Myquest_Command_Func002Func008001())then
			call DisplayTextToForce(GetForceOfPlayer(GetTriggerPlayer()),(udg_strings01[7]+("Your quest: train 5 units. Progress: "+(I2S(udg_integers13[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))])+"/5."))))
		endif
		if(Trig_Myquest_Command_Func002Func009001())then
			call DisplayTextToForce(GetForceOfPlayer(GetTriggerPlayer()),(udg_strings01[7]+("Your quest: kill 6 frogs. Progress: "+(I2S(udg_integers14[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))])+"/6."))))
		endif
		if(Trig_Myquest_Command_Func002Func010001())then
			call DisplayTextToForce(GetForceOfPlayer(GetTriggerPlayer()),(udg_strings01[7]+("Your quest: kill 6 stags. Progress: "+(I2S(udg_integers15[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))])+"/6."))))
		endif
		if(Trig_Myquest_Command_Func002Func011001())then
			call DisplayTextToForce(GetForceOfPlayer(GetTriggerPlayer()),(udg_strings01[7]+("Your quest: kill 6 raccoons. Progress: "+(I2S(udg_integers16[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))])+"/6."))))
		endif
		if(Trig_Myquest_Command_Func002Func012001())then
			call DisplayTextToForce(GetForceOfPlayer(GetTriggerPlayer()),(udg_strings01[7]+("Your quest: kill 6 rabbits. Progress: "+(I2S(udg_integers17[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))])+"/6."))))
		endif
		if(Trig_Myquest_Command_Func002Func013001())then
			call DisplayTextToForce(GetForceOfPlayer(GetTriggerPlayer()),(udg_strings01[7]+("Your quest: sell 6 items to the shop. Progress: "+(I2S(udg_integers18[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))])+"/6."))))
		endif
	endif
endfunction

function Trig_Quest_cancel_command_Func001001 takes nothing returns boolean
	return(udg_integers07[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))]==0)
endfunction

function Trig_Quest_cancel_command_Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
	return(udg_integers07[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))]>=1)
endfunction

function Trig_Quest_cancel_command_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
	if(Trig_Quest_cancel_command_Func001001())then
		call DisplayTextToForce(GetForceOfPlayer(GetTriggerPlayer()),(udg_strings01[7]+"You don't have a quest!|r"))
	endif
	if(Trig_Quest_cancel_command_Func002C())then
		call DisplayTextToForce(bj_FORCE_ALL_PLAYERS,(udg_strings01[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))]+(GetPlayerName(GetTriggerPlayer())+(udg_strings01[7]+" has canceled his quest."))))
		set udg_integers07[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))]=0
		set udg_booleans02[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))]=true
		call TriggerSleepAction(60.)
		call DisplayTextToForce(GetForceOfPlayer(GetTriggerPlayer()),(udg_strings01[7]+"El tiempo expir√≥, ya puedes pedir una nueva Quest.|r"))
		set udg_booleans02[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))]=false
	endif
endfunction

function Trig_quest_animal_dead_Func005C takes nothing returns boolean
	return(GetUnitTypeId(GetDyingUnit())=='n00A')or(GetUnitTypeId(GetDyingUnit())=='n009')or(GetUnitTypeId(GetDyingUnit())=='n008')or(GetUnitTypeId(GetDyingUnit())=='n00H')
endfunction

function Trig_quest_animal_dead_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
	return(GetOwningPlayer(GetDyingUnit())==Player($F))and(udg_integers07[(1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetKillingUnit())))]==1)and(Trig_quest_animal_dead_Func005C())
endfunction

function Trig_quest_animal_dead_Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
	return(udg_integers08[(1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetKillingUnit())))]==15)
endfunction

function Trig_quest_animal_dead_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
	set udg_integers08[(1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetKillingUnit())))]=(udg_integers08[(1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetKillingUnit())))]+1)
	if(Trig_quest_animal_dead_Func002C())then
		set udg_integer17=GetRandomInt($96,300)
		set udg_integer18=GetRandomInt($96,300)
		set udg_integer24=GetRandomInt(150,250)
		call DisplayTextToForce(bj_FORCE_ALL_PLAYERS,(udg_strings01[(1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetKillingUnit())))]+(GetPlayerName(GetOwningPlayer(GetKillingUnit()))+(udg_strings01[7]+(" has succesfully completed a quest and received "+(I2S(udg_integer17)+(" gold, "+(I2S(udg_integer18)+(" lumber and "+(I2S(udg_integer24)+" quest points."))))))))))
		set udg_integers19[(1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetKillingUnit())))]=(udg_integers19[(1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetKillingUnit())))]+udg_integer24)
		set udg_integers07[(1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetKillingUnit())))]=0
		call AdjustPlayerStateBJ(udg_integer17,GetOwningPlayer(GetKillingUnit()),PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_GOLD)
		call AdjustPlayerStateBJ(udg_integer18,GetOwningPlayer(GetKillingUnit()),PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_LUMBER)
		set udg_integers20[(1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetKillingUnit())))]=(udg_integers20[(1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetKillingUnit())))]+1)
	endif
endfunction

function Trig_quest_zombies_dead_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
	set udg_integers10[(1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetKillingUnit())))]=(udg_integers10[(1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetKillingUnit())))]+1)

		set udg_integer17=GetRandomInt($96,300)

function Trig_Init_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
	set udg_integer19=30
	set udg_integer20=45
	set udg_integer21=20
	set udg_integer23=30
	call EnableTrigger(udg_trigger205)
	call DisplayTextToForce(bj_FORCE_ALL_PLAYERS,(udg_strings01[9]+"[Hero Upgrade System] If you want to upgrade your hero type -H."))
	call TriggerSleepAction(30.01)
	call DisplayTextToForce(bj_FORCE_ALL_PLAYERS,(udg_strings01[9]+"[Hero Upgrade System] If you want to upgrade your hero type -H."))
endfunction

function Trig_Hero_command_Func001001 takes nothing returns boolean
	return(IsUnitAliveBJ(udg_units01[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))])==false)
endfunction

function Trig_Hero_command_Func002001 takes nothing returns boolean
	return(udg_boolean03)
endfunction

function Trig_Hero_command_Func003C takes nothing returns boolean
	return(IsUnitAliveBJ(udg_units01[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))]))and(udg_boolean03==false)
endfunction

function Trig_Hero_command_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
	if(Trig_Hero_command_Func001001())then
		call DisplayTextToForce(GetForceOfPlayer(GetTriggerPlayer()),(udg_strings01[9]+"Your hero is dead or you don't have a hero."))
	endif
	if(Trig_Hero_command_Func002001())then
		call DisplayTextToForce(GetForceOfPlayer(GetTriggerPlayer()),(udg_strings01[9]+"Someone is currently upgradeing his hero, please wait and try again later."))
	endif
	if(Trig_Hero_command_Func003C())then
		set udg_booleans03[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))]=true
		set udg_boolean03=true
		call DialogClear(udg_dialog02)
		call DialogSetMessage(udg_dialog02,("Hero Upgrade Center ("+(udg_strings01[$A]+(I2S(udg_integers19[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))])+"|r quest points)"))))
		call DialogAddButtonBJ(udg_dialog02,("+12 Damage ("+(I2S((GetPlayerTechCountSimple('R00F',GetTriggerPlayer())*udg_integer19))+" quest points)")))
		set udg_buttons02[1]=bj_lastCreatedButton
		call DialogAddButtonBJ(udg_dialog02,("+250 Health ("+(I2S((GetPlayerTechCountSimple('R00G',GetTriggerPlayer())*udg_integer20))+" quest points)")))
		set udg_buttons02[2]=bj_lastCreatedButton
		call DialogAddButtonBJ(udg_dialog02,("+3 Armor ("+(I2S((GetPlayerTechCountSimple('R00H',GetTriggerPlayer())*udg_integer21))+" quest points)")))
		set udg_buttons02[3]=bj_lastCreatedButton
		call DialogAddButtonBJ(udg_dialog02,("+75 Mana ("+(I2S((GetPlayerTechCountSimple('R00I',GetTriggerPlayer())*udg_integer23))+" quest points)")))
		set udg_buttons02[4]=bj_lastCreatedButton
		call DialogAddButtonBJ(udg_dialog02,"Exit")
		set udg_buttons02[5]=bj_lastCreatedButton
		call DialogDisplayBJ(true,udg_dialog02,GetTriggerPlayer())
	endif
endfunction

function Trig_Hero_1_button_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
	return(GetClickedButton()==udg_buttons02[1])
endfunction

function Trig_Hero_1_button_Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
	return(udg_integers19[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))]<(GetPlayerTechCountSimple('R00F',GetTriggerPlayer())*udg_integer19))
endfunction

function Trig_Hero_1_button_Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
	return(IsUnitAliveBJ(udg_units01[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))])==false)
endfunction

function Trig_Hero_1_button_Func003C takes nothing returns boolean
	return(udg_integers19[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))]>=(GetPlayerTechCountSimple('R00F',GetTriggerPlayer())*udg_integer19))and(IsUnitAliveBJ(udg_units01[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))]))
endfunction

function Trig_Hero_1_button_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
	if(Trig_Hero_1_button_Func001C())then
		call DisplayTextToForce(GetForceOfPlayer(GetTriggerPlayer()),(udg_strings01[9]+"You don't have enough quest points!|r"))
		set udg_boolean03=false
		set udg_booleans03[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))]=false
	endif
	if(Trig_Hero_1_button_Func002C())then
		call DisplayTextToForce(GetForceOfPlayer(GetTriggerPlayer()),(udg_strings01[9]+"Your hero is dead!|r"))
		set udg_boolean03=false
		set udg_booleans03[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))]=false
	endif
	if(Trig_Hero_1_button_Func003C())then
		set udg_integer22=(GetPlayerTechCountSimple('R00F',GetTriggerPlayer())*udg_integer19)
		set udg_integers19[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))]=(udg_integers19[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))]-udg_integer22)
		call SetPlayerTechResearchedSwap('R00F',(GetPlayerTechCountSimple('R00F',GetTriggerPlayer())+1),GetTriggerPlayer())
		call DisplayTextToForce(GetForceOfPlayer(GetTriggerPlayer()),(udg_strings01[9]+("You have upgraded the damage of the hero to level "+(I2S(GetPlayerTechCountSimple('R00F',GetTriggerPlayer()))+(" for "+(I2S(udg_integer22)+" quest points."))))))
		call DialogClear(udg_dialog02)
		call DialogSetMessage(udg_dialog02,("Hero Upgrade Center ("+(udg_strings01[$A]+(I2S(udg_integers19[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))])+"|r quest points)"))))
		call DialogAddButtonBJ(udg_dialog02,("+12 Damage ("+(I2S((GetPlayerTechCountSimple('R00F',GetTriggerPlayer())*udg_integer19))+" quest points)")))
		set udg_buttons02[1]=bj_lastCreatedButton
		call DialogAddButtonBJ(udg_dialog02,("+250 Health ("+(I2S((GetPlayerTechCountSimple('R00G',GetTriggerPlayer())*udg_integer20))+" quest points)")))
		set udg_buttons02[2]=bj_lastCreatedButton
		call DialogAddButtonBJ(udg_dialog02,("+3 Armor ("+(I2S((GetPlayerTechCountSimple('R00H',GetTriggerPlayer())*udg_integer21))+" quest points)")))
		set udg_buttons02[3]=bj_lastCreatedButton
		call DialogAddButtonBJ(udg_dialog02,("+75 Mana ("+(I2S((GetPlayerTechCountSimple('R00I',GetTriggerPlayer())*udg_integer23))+" quest points)")))
		set udg_buttons02[4]=bj_lastCreatedButton
		call DialogAddButtonBJ(udg_dialog02,"Exit")
		set udg_buttons02[5]=bj_lastCreatedButton
		call DialogDisplayBJ(true,udg_dialog02,GetTriggerPlayer())
	endif
endfunction

		call DisplayTextToForce(GetForceOfPlayer(GetTriggerPlayer()),(udg_strings01[9]+("You have upgraded the mana of the hero to level "+(I2S(GetPlayerTechCountSimple('R00I',GetTriggerPlayer()))+(" for "+(I2S(udg_integer22)+" quest points."))))))
		call DialogClear(udg_dialog02)
		call DialogSetMessage(udg_dialog02,("Hero Upgrade Center ("+(udg_strings01[$A]+(I2S(udg_integers19[(1+GetPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()))])+"|r quest points)"))))
		call DialogAddButtonBJ(udg_dialog02,("+12 Damage ("+(I2S((GetPlayerTechCountSimple('R00F',GetTriggerPlayer())*udg_integer19))+" quest points)")))
		set udg_buttons02[1]=bj_lastCreatedButton
		call DialogAddButtonBJ(udg_dialog02,("+250 Health ("+(I2S((GetPlayerTechCountSimple('R00G',GetTriggerPlayer())*udg_integer20))+" quest points)")))
		set udg_buttons02[2]=bj_lastCreatedButton
		call DialogAddButtonBJ(udg_dialog02,("+3 Armor ("+(I2S((GetPlayerTechCountSimple('R00H',GetTriggerPlayer())*udg_integer21))+" quest points)")))
		set udg_buttons02[3]=bj_lastCreatedButton
		call DialogAddButtonBJ(udg_dialog02,("+75 Mana ("+(I2S((GetPlayerTechCountSimple('R00I',GetTriggerPlayer())*udg_integer23))+" quest points)")))
		set udg_buttons02[4]=bj_lastCreatedButton
		call DialogAddButtonBJ(udg_dialog02,"Exit")
		set udg_buttons02[5]=bj_lastCreatedButton
		call DialogDisplayBJ(true,udg_dialog02,GetTriggerPlayer())
	endif
endfunction

function Trig_Wolf_create_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
	call DisplayTextToForce(GetForceOfPlayer(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit())),(udg_strings01[$A]+"Debido a que desarrollaste el 1¬™er Tier llamado Skeletal Longevity upgrade, has recibido a un Lobo con habilidades extraordinarias.|r"))
	call DisplayTextToForce(GetForceOfPlayer(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit())),(udg_strings01[$A]+"Si quieres ver el nivel de habilidades del lobo escribe -mywolf.|r"))
	call DisplayTextToForce(GetForceOfPlayer(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit())),(udg_strings01[$A]+"Para fortalecer a tu lobo puedes alimentarlo con (Ribs/Meat/Food) incluso puede llevar inventario."))
	call DisplayTextToForce(GetForceOfPlayer(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit())),(udg_strings01[$A]+"Sin embargo... si tu lobo muere definitivamente a causa de tu primera muerte con el h√©roe... cagaste viteh"))
	if(Trig_Wolf_create_Func004C())then
		call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1,'H01D',GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()),GetUnitLoc(udg_units01[(1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit())))]),bj_UNIT_FACING)
		set udg_integers24[(1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit())))]=1
		set udg_integers25[(1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit())))]=1
		set udg_integers26[(1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit())))]=1
		set udg_integers27[(1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit())))]=1
		set udg_integers29[(1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit())))]=1
		set udg_booleans04[(1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit())))]=true
		set udg_integers30[(1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit())))]=4
	endif
endfunction

function Trig_Wolf_dead_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
	if(Trig_Wolf_dead_Func001C())then
		call DisplayTextToForce(GetForceOfPlayer(GetOwningPlayer(GetDyingUnit())),(udg_strings01[$A]+"KAJ que gay.. tu lobo muri√≥. Revivir√° en 60 segundos."))
		call TriggerSleepAction(60.)
		if(Trig_Wolf_dead_Func001Func003C())then
			call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1,'H01D',GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()),GetUnitLoc(udg_units01[(1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit())))]),bj_UNIT_FACING)
			call DisplayTextToForce(GetForceOfPlayer(GetOwningPlayer(GetDyingUnit())),(udg_strings01[$A]+"Your wolf was respawned at your hero."))
			call SetUnitAbilityLevelSwapped('S000',bj_lastCreatedUnit,udg_integers24[(1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetDyingUnit())))])
			call SetUnitAbilityLevelSwapped('A05B',bj_lastCreatedUnit,udg_integers25[(1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetDyingUnit())))])
			call SetUnitAbilityLevelSwapped('A05C',bj_lastCreatedUnit,udg_integers26[(1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetDyingUnit())))])
			call SetUnitAbilityLevelSwapped('A05A',bj_lastCreatedUnit,udg_integers27[(1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetDyingUnit())))])
			call SetUnitAbilityLevelSwapped('A05D',bj_lastCreatedUnit,udg_integers29[(1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetDyingUnit())))])
		endif
	endif
endfunction

function Trig_Wolf_Upgrade_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
	if(Trig_Wolf_Upgrade_Func002C())then
		set udg_integers30[(1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetSpellAbilityUnit())))]=(udg_integers30[(1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetSpellAbilityUnit())))]-1)
		call DisplayTextToForce(GetForceOfPlayer(GetOwningPlayer(GetSpellAbilityUnit())),(udg_strings01[$A]+("Feed your wolf for "+(I2S(udg_integers30[(1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetSpellAbilityUnit())))])+" times to level up your wolf."))))
		if(Trig_Wolf_Upgrade_Func002Func003C())then
			call SetPlayerTechResearchedSwap('R00K',(GetPlayerTechCountSimple('R00K',GetOwningPlayer(GetSpellAbilityUnit()))+1),GetOwningPlayer(GetSpellAbilityUnit()))
			set udg_integers30[(1+GetPlayerId(GetOwningPlayer(GetSpellAbilityUnit())))]=4
			call DisplayTextToForce(GetForceOfPlayer(GetOwningPlayer(GetSpellAbilityUnit())),(udg_strings01[$A]+"You have upgraded your wolf."))
		endif
		if(Trig_Wolf_Upgrade_Func002Func004001())then
			call RemoveItem(GetItemOfTypeFromUnitBJ(GetSpellAbilityUnit(),'I00W'))
		endif
		if(Trig_Wolf_Upgrade_Func002Func005001())then
			call RemoveItem(GetItemOfTypeFromUnitBJ(GetSpellAbilityUnit(),'I03Q'))
		endif
		if(Trig_Wolf_Upgrade_Func002Func006001())then
			call RemoveItem(GetItemOfTypeFromUnitBJ(GetSpellAbilityUnit(),'I00V'))
		endif
	endif
	if(Trig_Wolf_Upgrade_Func003C())then
		call DisplayTextToForce(GetForceOfPlayer(GetOwningPlayer(GetSpellAbilityUnit())),(udg_strings01[$A]+"You can use meat only on your wolf!"))
	endif
endfunction

function Trig_Gate_init_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
	call SetDestructableInvulnerable(udg_destructable07,true)
	call SetDestructableInvulnerable(udg_destructable08,true)
	call SetDestructableInvulnerable(udg_destructable09,true)
	call SetDestructableInvulnerable(udg_destructable01,true)
	call SetDestructableInvulnerable(udg_destructable02,true)
	call SetDestructableInvulnerable(udg_destructable12,true)
	call SetDestructableInvulnerable(udg_destructable11,true)
	call SetDestructableInvulnerable(udg_destructable10,true)
	call ModifyGateBJ(1,udg_destructable10)
	call ModifyGateBJ(1,udg_destructable11)
	call ModifyGateBJ(1,udg_destructable12)
	call ModifyGateBJ(1,udg_destructable07)
	call ModifyGateBJ(1,udg_destructable08)
	call ModifyGateBJ(1,udg_destructable09)
	call ModifyGateBJ(1,udg_destructable01)
	call ModifyGateBJ(1,udg_destructable02)
endfunction

function Trig_Gate_Cllose_when_tower_dies_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
	call TriggerSleepAction(.01)
	call DisplayTextToForce(bj_FORCE_ALL_PLAYERS,(udg_strings01[1]+"All gates near the Zombie Tower will be closed for 15 seconds!"))
	call ModifyGateBJ(0,udg_destructable09)
	call ModifyGateBJ(0,udg_destructable08)
	call ModifyGateBJ(0,udg_destructable07)
	call DisableTrigger(GetTriggeringTrigger())
	call TriggerSleepAction(15.)
	call EnableTrigger(GetTriggeringTrigger())
	call ModifyGateBJ(1,udg_destructable09)
	call ModifyGateBJ(1,udg_destructable08)
	call ModifyGateBJ(1,udg_destructable07)
endfunction

function Trig_Gates_Cllose_when_tower_dies_2_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
	call TriggerSleepAction(.01)
	call ModifyGateBJ(0,udg_destructable01)
	call ModifyGateBJ(0,udg_destructable02)
	call DisplayTextToForce(bj_FORCE_ALL_PLAYERS,(udg_strings01[1]+"All gates near the Zombie Tower will be closed for 15 seconds!"))
	call DisableTrigger(GetTriggeringTrigger())
	call TriggerSleepAction(15.)
	call EnableTrigger(GetTriggeringTrigger())
	call ModifyGateBJ(1,udg_destructable01)
	call ModifyGateBJ(1,udg_destructable02)
endfunction

function InitCustomTriggers2 takes nothing returns nothing
	set udg_trigger01=CreateTrigger()
	call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(udg_trigger01,EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_SPELL_CAST)
	call TriggerAddCondition(udg_trigger01,Condition(function Trig_CF_Cast_Conditions))
